name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Queen Room
info:Stayed in September 2023

rating:1
posted:Posted October 3, 2023
msg:Because it was the first time for me to bring my girlfriend to Changsha, I wanted to make her feel better in all aspects, so I chose a relatively old hotel that I thought was more reliable. As a person in Changsha, it was also the first time for me to stay at Huaya, but I didn't expect the experience to be so bad. What I regretted most was that I stayed there for two consecutive days. It was really a lesson learned.
First of all, I chose a non-smoking floor. As a result, when we returned to the hotel last night, there was a Hetianxia cigarette butt right under our door that came from nowhere, which made us rush into the room to check if there were any items missing. We called the hotel to report this phenomenon, but there was no feedback. The next day, they called us to ask if we wanted to extend our stay. This made us feel that this hotel was so unsafe, and there was no basic service.

Secondly, there were people making noises outside the door at 8 or 9 in the morning for two consecutive days. The noises of children making noises and aunts disturbing the room were particularly loud. It made it impossible for people to sleep in.

It was really a bit disappointing. I might as well stay in another hotel if I spend four or five hundred yuan a night.
